'qi'ruo'wang'ming'he 其若王命何

'yi'zhi'jian'shi'ren'zong'huang'di 以直谏事仁宗皇帝
'yi'zhi'jin'qiu'zui'gao 以至近求最高
'yi'zhi'jin'ri 以至今日
'yi'zhi'qi'xing'yan'er 以致其性焉尔
'yi'zhi'qi'yin'si 以致其禋祀
'yi'zhi'rong'yu'shang'mu 以致戎于商牧
'yi'zhi'shi'guo 以之事国
'yi'zhi'suo'bu'gan'chu'ye 义之所不敢出也
'yi'zhi'tai'yue 易之泰曰
'yi'zhi'tian'di'zhi'guang'da 以知天地之广大
'yi'zhi'tian'xia'zhi'shi 以致天下之士
'yi'zhi'wang'yi 亦知亡矣
'yi'zhi'wei'gong'zhi'wei'ren'yi'hu 亦知威公之为人矣乎
'yi'zhi'wei'ren 以之为人
'yi'zhi'wei'shen 一之为甚
'yi'zhi'wei'tian'xia'guo'jia 以之为天下国家
'yi'zhi'wei'xin 以之为心
'yi'zhi'wu'guo 以志吾过
'yi'zhi'xiu'shen 以之修身
'yi'zhi'yu'cheng'wei'xie'zheng'zhi'bian'ye 以至于诚伪邪正之辨也
'yi'zhi'yu'qi'chang'duan'xiao'da'mei'e 以至于其长短小大美恶
'yi'zhi'yu'si 以至于死
'yi'zhi'yuan'yu'qi'pian 亦治园于其偏
'yi'zhi'zhi'da'ji'ru'gu 一指之大几如股
'yi'zhong'bi'yi'zhi'zui 以重敝邑之罪
'yi'zhong'de'zui'yu'xia'zhi'shi 以重得罪于下执事
'yi'zhong'hou'zhi'zhi'ye 亦忠厚之至也
'yi'zhong'qi'zi'sun 以种其子孙
'yi'zhou'pi'bi 益州疲敝
'yi'zhu'cuo'wei'ming 以诛错为名
'yi'zhu'dan'qi'jian 倚柱弹其剑
'yi'zhu'tian'di'yin'yang'si'shi'wu'xing 易著天地阴阳四时五行
'yi'zhui'nian'qian'xun 以追念前勋
'yi'zhuo'gao'ke 已擢高科
'yi'zi'bu'chi 亦自不斥
'yi'zi'cheng'ren 已自成人
'yi'zi'di'zhi'chu'mo 以恣敌之出没
'yi'zi'er'shi'zhi 易子而食之
'yi'zi'hui'zui'yu'che'chen'ma'zu'zhi 以自悔罪于车尘马足之
'yi'zi'jiang'zhi'zhi'wei 以自将之至危
'yi'zi'qiu'zhi'sheng 以兹丘之胜
'yi'zi'shang'ye 以自伤也
'yi'zi'wei'tuo'tuo'yun 亦自谓橐驼云
'yi'zi'xiang'tu'mie 以自相屠灭
'yi'zi'zhi'dao 以子之道
'yi'zi'zou'shan'dao 以咨诹善道
'yi'zu'xia'du'gu'ren'shu 以足下读古人书
'yi'zu'yi'chang'xu'you'qing 亦足以畅叙幽情
'yi'zu'yi'cheng'kuai'shi'su 亦足以称快世俗
'yi'zu'yi'fu'le 亦足以富乐
'yi'zu'zhi'qi'zhi'zhi'suo'cun 亦足知其志之所存
'yi'zui'ye 亦罪也
'yi'zuo'you'xian'wei'zhi'rong'ye 以左右先为之容也
'yin'bi 淫嬖
'yin'bu'guo'er'dou'jing'zui'yi 饮不过二斗径醉矣
'yin'chan'zhi'yue 因谗之曰
'yin'chang'er'bei 隐长而卑
'yin'chang'you'xian 隐长又贤
'yin'cheng'yi'wei'tai'zhe'jiu'yi 因城以为台者旧矣
'yin'dao'qi'sheng'shi'yi'bei'qi'shuai 因道其盛时以悲其衰
'yin'de'guan'suo'wei'shi'zhong'zhe 因得观所谓石钟者
'yin'de'jin'jiao'dang'shi'zhi'xian'hao 因得尽交当世之贤豪
'yin'de'yi'zi'wan'yu'qi'jian'yi 因得以自完于其间矣
'yin'de'zhi'shi 隐德之士
'yin'er'jia'li'zhi 因而贾利之
'yin'er'qu'zhi 因而去之
'yin'er'yu'zhi 因而予之
'yin'feng'nu'hao 阴风怒号
'yin'he'wei'chi 因河为池
'yin'he'zhi'hui'ru'che'lun 阴壑之虺如车轮
'yin'hu'shang'yi'zi'zhuo 引壶觞以自酌
'yin'jiu'yu'si'ting'er'le'zhi 饮酒于斯亭而乐之
'yin'ke'ba'dou'er'zui'er'can 饮可八斗而醉二参
'yin'ke'wu'liu'dou'jing'zui'yi 饮可五六斗径醉矣
'yin'li'cheng'bian 因利乘便
'yin'liu'huai'wang 因留怀王
'yin'liu'zhong'shu 引流种树
'yin'luan'qi'xin 淫乱其心
'yin'ming'yu'ji'zhi 因命余记之
'yin'ping'yuan'jun'wei'zhao'wang'yue 因平原君谓赵王曰
'yin'po'yi 淫破义
'yin'qi'bao'bian'zhi'yi'yi'zhi'shang'fa 因其褒贬之义以制赏罚
'yin'qi'di 因其地
'yin'qi'fu'hou 因其富厚
'yin'qi'tu'su 因其土俗
'yin'qie'shi'xi'shou'er'kang 饮且食兮寿而康
'yin'qin'shen'hou 殷勤甚厚
'yin'ran'ru'cheng'guo 隐然如城郭
'yin'ran'ru'da'huan 隐然如大环
'yin'ren'er'ling 因人而灵
'yin'ren'zhi'li'er'bi'zhi 因人之力而敝之
'yin'ru'xi'liu 饮茹溪流
'yin'shang'ke'yu 引商刻羽
'yin'shao'qi'quan 因烧其券
'yin'shao'zhe'zui 饮少辄醉
'yin'she'qi'ming 因舍其名
'yin'shi'bi'ji 饮食必祭
'yin'shi'bi'zhu'yue 饮食必祝曰
'yin'shi'er'qu'zhi 引师而去之
'yin'si'wei'tian 殷祀未殄
'yin'suo'yu'qi'jia 因索于其家
'yin'tian'xia'zhi'shi'wang 因天下之失望
'yin'tian'zhi'zhu 因天之助
'yin'tu'hou'fang'zhi'bi 阴图后房之嬖
'yin'wei'ben'qi'shan'chuan 因为本其山川
'yin'wei'gong'zhi'wen 因威公之问
'yin'wei'jiao 引微缴
'yin'wei'wu'shang 因为诬上
'yin'wei'zhi'fang'shan'zi 因谓之方山子
'yin'wu'xing'gan 因物兴感
'yin'wu'ze'shan'yue'beng'tui 喑呜则山岳崩颓
'yin'xiao'cheng'qun 吟啸成群
'yin'xiao'wei'mai'yue 因笑谓迈曰
'yin'yang'zhi'bian 阴阳之变
'yin'ye 淫也
'yin'yi'ce 因遗策
'yin'yi'sheng'dui'qin'bo 阴饴甥对秦伯
'yin'yi'wei'hao'yan 因以为号焉
'yin'yi'wei'liu'shang'qu'shui 引以为流觞曲水
'yin'yi'yi'qi'shi'yun 因以遗其世云
'yin'you'ren'ren'yue'ji'zi 殷有仁人曰箕子
'yin'yu'hun'hei 阴雨昏黑
'yin'yu'shi'yan'er'ci'li 隐于是焉而辞立
'yin'yu'shi'yi 引喻失义
'yin'yu'shou'yang'shan 隐于首阳山
'yin'yu'yu'ma'shang'lun'yong'bing'ji'gu 因与余马上论用兵及古
'yin'ze'wang'shan 淫则忘善
'yin'zhe'zhi'suo'pan'xuan 隐者之所盘旋
'yin'zhi'ce'xun 饮至策勋
'yin'zhi'er'tan'yue 因指而叹曰
'yin'zhi'xing'ye'yi'you'song 殷之兴也以有娀
'yin'zhu'miao'yi'zhi'qing 因诸苗夷之请
'yin'zhui'zi'ci'qi'gu 引锥自刺其股
'yin'zuo'shi'yi'wei'zhi 因作诗以遗之
'yin'zuo'xiao'lou'er'jian 因作小楼二间
'ying'chi'er'qu'jin'qi'zhi 盈尺而曲尽其制
'ying'dai'zuo'you 映带左右
'ying'dui'zhu'hou 应对诸侯
'ying'jian'shu'yu'song 迎蹇叔于宋
'ying'jun'dao'zhong 迎君道中
'ying'kao'shu 颍考叔
'ying'kao'shu'qu'zheng'bo'zhi'qi'mao'hu 颍考叔取郑伯之旗蝥弧
'ying'kao'shu'wei'ying'gu'feng'ren 颍考叔为颍谷封人
'ying'kao'shu'yue 颍考叔曰
'ying'ke'mu'shi'yu'ren'shu 应科目时与人书
'ying'liang'er'jing'cong 赢粮而景从
'ying'shang'ren'ye 颍上人也
'ying'shi'zhi'zhong 营室之中
'ying'su'yue 迎素月
'ying'sui'bu'ren 婴虽不仁
'ying'xiong'jun'jie'zhan'gong'zhu'shou'zhi'ji 英雄俊杰战攻驻守之迹
'ying'xiong'shi'lu'tuo'zu'wu'men'zhi'bei 英雄失路托足无门之悲
'ying'xu'yi'fu 盈虚倚伏
'ying'xu'zhe'ru'bi 盈虚者如彼
'ying'ying'zhi'sheng'yu'er'mou 瀯瀯之声与耳谋
'ying'yu'yu'men 萦纡郁闷
'ying'zhi'yi'shou 应之以手
'yong'cai'ru'fen'tu 用财如粪土
'yong'da'gai 拥大盖
'yong'dai'tao'wa 用代陶瓦
'yong'er'bu'kui 用而不匮
'yong'er'bu'tong 壅而不通
'yong'er'wu'suo'cheng'ye 用而无所成也
'yong'guang'yin'si 用广殷祀
'yong'gui'yu'zhi'zheng'zhe 用规于执政者
'yong'he'jiu'nian 永和九年
'yong'ji'wo'wen'gong 用集我文公
'yong'ji'ze'tong 壅极则通
'yong'ju'zhi'you'li'zhe'bu'ai'qi'qiong 庸讵知有力者不哀其穷
'yong'ju'zhi'yu'xiao'hu 庸讵止于笑乎
'yong'jun'zhi'xin 用君之心
'yong'jun'zi'zhi'zhen'peng 用君子之真朋
'yong'le'yi'lai'ru'yang'shi'qi'yang'rong 永乐以来如杨士奇杨荣
'yong'li'ru'ci 用力如此
'yong'li'yu'dang'shi'zhe'zhi'suo'wei'ye 用力于当世者之所为也
'yong'li'yue'gong 用力曰功
'yong'li'zhe'shi'yu'ren 用力者使于人
'yong'ling'xi 永陵喜
'yong'ling'ying'zhu 永陵英主
'yong'lv'he'le 永履和乐
'yong'neng'xie'yu'shang'xia 用能协于上下
'yong'qi'ben'yu 勇期贲育
'yong'qi'ren'fan'jian 用齐人反间
'yong'qi'ye 勇气也
'yong'qie 勇怯
'yong'ren'bu'jin'qi'suo'yu'wei 用人不尽其所欲为
'yong'ren'ru'zi'jie'de'yi'er'wu'zhi 庸人孺子皆得易而侮之
'yong'wei'guo'dian 永为国典
'yong'wei'sheng'shi 用为圣师
'yong'wu'zhi'di'ye 用武之地也
'yong'xi'er'lei 永锡尔类
'yong'xin'zhe'shi'ren 用心者使人
'yong'yong'zhou'zhi'di 拥雍州之地
'yong'yu'gan'wei 勇于敢为
'yong'yu'shi 咏于诗
'yong'yu'wei'ren 勇于为人
'yong'zhe'jie'qi'li 勇者竭其力
'yong'zhi'bu'jie 用之不竭
'yong'zhi'jue'ye 勇之决也
'yong'zhi'ren'zheng'ben'zou'yan 永之人争奔走焉
'yong'zhi'ru'ni'sha 用之如泥沙
'yong'zhi'suo'qu'yi'ye 用之所趣异也
'yong'zhou'shi'wei'jiu'yi'zhi'lu 永州实惟九疑之麓
'yong'zhou'wei'shi'jun'xin'tang'ji 永州韦使君新堂记
'yong'zhou'zhi'di 雍州之地
'yong'zhou'zhi'ye'chan'yi'she 永州之野产异蛇
'you'ai'qi'su'zhi'an'xian 又爱其俗之安闲
'you'ai'yan'zi'zhi'ren'you'deng'ji 又爱晏子之仁有等级
'you'an'de'qin'qin'xiang'chou'ye 又安得亲亲相仇也
'you'an'gan'du'xie 又安敢毒邪
'you'an'neng'yi'hao'hao'zhi'bai'er'meng 又安能以皓皓之白而蒙
'you'an'yi'lai'er'bai'nian 有庵以来二百年
'you'an'zhi'chen'zhi'suo'wei'zai 又安知臣之所为哉
'you'an'zhi'fu'bei'zong'er'qu'ye 又安知夫被纵而去也
'you'ba'er'qi'zhi 有拔而起之
'you'ba'nian 又八年
'you'bai'tou'ru'xin 有白头如新
'you'bao'chan'shan'ji 游褒禅山记
'you'bei'pu'dao 有碑仆道
'you'bei'yue'liang'yi'dian 又北曰两仪殿
'you'ben'you'yuan 有本有原
'you'bi'zhi'si 有鼻之祀
'you'bian'sui'wu'guang'zhe 有卞随务光者
'you'bing'xiang'ye 又兵象也
'you'bu'dang'shu'fu'zhi 又不当束缚之
'you'bu'de'hao 犹不得好
'you'bu'de'jian'zhe 有不得见者
'you'bu'de'yi'zhe'er'hou'yan 有不得已者而后言
'you'bu'de'zhao'xi'ji'jian 又不得朝夕继见
'you'bu'gong'ze'xiu'ming 有不贡则修名
'you'bu'huo'wen'ming 又不获闻命
'you'bu'ji'ze'xiu'yi 有不祭则修意
'you'bu'ke'bu'wang'zhe 有不可不忘者
'you'bu'ke'bu'zhi'zhe 有不可不知者
'you'bu'ke'wang'zhe 有不可忘者
'you'bu'ke'yi'wu'jing 又不可以武竞
'you'bu'neng'bei'qi'gong 又不能备其工
'you'bu'neng'bu'yi'zhi'xing'huai 犹不能不以之兴怀
'you'bu'neng'cheng'da'xun 又不能成大勋
'you'bu'neng'jin'ye 犹不能禁也
'you'bu'neng'shi'wu'gong'zhi'zun 犹不能恃无功之尊
'you'bu'neng'shi'yi'bu'que 又不能拾遗补阙
'you'bu'neng'wei'hai 犹不能为害
'you'bu'neng'xuan'jin'qi'yi 犹不能宣尽其意

'you'bu'ning'yi'qin'shu'fu 又不佞以勤叔父
'you'bu'ping'zhi'xin 有不平之心
'you'bu'ran'ye 又不然也
'you'bu'ru'fu'zi'zhi'pin'jian 有不如夫子之贫贱
'you'bu'ru'ren 犹不如人
'you'bu'si'ze'xiu'yan 有不祀则修言
'you'bu'wang'ze'xiu'de 有不王则修德

'you'bu'xiang'ze'xiu'wen 有不享则修文
'you'bu'yi'qi'suo'yi'ran 又不易其所以然
'you'bu'yu'zhi'bei 有不虞之备
